## 1. LLM响应解析器优化与测试增强 - 小沈-2026-04-18

### 1.1 主要改进

从v0.9.8.4到v0.9.8.5的变更包括：

1. **LLM响应解析器重构优化** (ec444867)
   - 简化_extract_json_block()函数，移除冗余的状态处理逻辑
   - 新增_create_action_result()函数，添加完整的参数校验和错误恢复
   - 优化_determine_parse_type()函数，添加统一的异常处理机制
   - 新增_extract_tool_params_from_thought()函数，完善fallback机制
   - 添加尾随逗号自动修复功能
   - 完善所有函数的文档说明

2. **测试用例增强** (ec444867)
   - 新增11个测试用例，覆盖新增函数和边界情况
   - 新增真实LLM输出数据验证测试
   - 所有82个测试全部通过，无回归问题

3. **LLM解析器设计文档更新** (a0fade35)
   - 删除重复内容，优化文档结构
   - 新增深度综合分析章节
   - 代码修正和文档同步更新

4. **Git忽略规则更新** (未提交的修改)
   - 添加.arts/目录到.gitignore

### 1.2 质量保证

- 无新错误产生
- 无功能丢失
- 代码质量显著提升
- 异常处理更加健壮

def get_stream_error_info(error_type: str, original_message: str = None) -> tuple[str, str]:
    # 鑾峰彇閿欒鐮?
    error_code, default_message = ERROR_TYPE_MAP.get(error_type, ('server', '鏈嶅姟璋冪敤澶辫触'))
    
    # 浼樺厛浣跨敤鍘熷閿欒娑堟伅

    return error_code, message
```

### 1.3 鏂板嚱鏁板姛鑳?

## 1. 淇chat_stream()鏂规硶429閿欒澶勭悊 - 灏忔矆-2026-03-29

### 1.1 闂鑳屾櫙

鐢ㄦ埛楠屾敹鍙戠幇锛氬綋429闄愭祦鍙戠敓鏃讹紝TextStrategy杩斿洖绌哄唴瀹癸紝閿欒鎻愮ず娌℃湁鏄剧ず銆?

### 1.2 闂鏍瑰洜

鍦?`llm_core.py` 鐨?`chat_stream()` 鏂规硶涓紝褰?HTTP 鐘舵€佺爜涓嶆槸 200 鏃讹紙绗?67-169琛岋級锛?
```python
if response.status_code != 200:
    yield StreamChunk(content="", model=self.model, is_done=True)
    return
```

**闂**锛氭病鏈変粠鍝嶅簲浣撲腑鎻愬彇閿欒淇℃伅骞惰缃?`stream_error`锛?

### 1.3 淇鍐呭

**淇敼鏂囦欢**: `backend/app/services/llm_core.py`

鍦?`response.status_code != 200` 鏃讹紝浠庡搷搴斾綋涓彁鍙栭敊璇俊鎭細
```python
if response.status_code != 200:
    error_body = ""
    try:
        error_body = await response.aread()
        error_text = error_body.decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
        logger.error(f"[chat_stream] HTTP {response.status_code} error response: {error_text[:500]}")
        try:
            error_json = json.loads(error_text)
            error_msg = error_json.get("error", {}).get("message", "")
            if error_msg:
                yield StreamChunk(content="", model=self.model, is_done=True, 
                    stream_error=f"API Error: {response.status_code}, {error_msg}",
                    stream_error_type="api_error")
                return
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            pass
        yield StreamChunk(content="", model=self.model, is_done=True,
            stream_error=f"HTTP {response.status_code}: {error_text[:200]}",
            stream_error_type="http_error")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[chat_stream] Failed to read error response: {e}")
        yield StreamChunk(content="", model=self.model, is_done=True,
            stream_error=f"HTTP {response.status_code} error",
            stream_error_type="http_error")
    return
```

### 1.3 淇鍐呭

```python
# 銆愪慨澶?2026-03-29銆戝鐞?LLM 杩斿洖绾枃鏈紙濡?"I will now summarize..."锛夌殑鎯呭喌
# 褰撴棤娉曟彁鍙栧嚭缁撴瀯鍖?action 鏃讹紝妫€鏌ユ槸鍚︽槸鎬荤粨鎬ф枃鏈紝濡傛灉鏄垯杩斿洖 finish
summarize_patterns = [
    r'(?:summarize|summary|鎬荤粨|I have found|I will)',
    r'(?:宸插畬鎴恷浠诲姟瀹屾垚|瀹屾垚浜?',
    r'(?:鏍规嵁.*?缁撴灉|鍩轰簬.*?鍐呭)',

## 2. 褰诲簳淇 step 璁℃暟鍣ㄧ粺涓€闂 - 灏忔矆-2026-03-23

### 1.1 闂鎻忚堪

鏂囦欢鎿嶄綔寮傚父鏃讹紝error 姝ラ缂栧彿璺冲彿銆備緥濡傦細
- start: step=1
- error: step=3 (璺宠繃浜?step=2)

    code: str,
    message: str,
    error_type: str,
    step_num: int,
    model: Optional[str] = None,
    provider: Optional[str] = None
) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """鍒涘缓淇濆瓨鍒版暟鎹簱鐨?error_step"""

        'model': model,
        'provider': provider
    }

## 1. 淇 final/error 姝ラ step 澶?1 鐨勯棶棰?- 灏忔矆-2026-03-23

### 1.2 鏍瑰洜鍒嗘瀽

### 1.4 璁捐鑳屾櫙

### 1.8 LongCat Function Calling 璋冪敤楠岃瘉

**API璇锋眰鏍煎紡**锛?
```json
{
  "model": "longcat-xxx",
  "messages": [...],
  "tools": [
    {
      "type": "function",
      "function": {
        "name": "list_directory",
        "description": "...",
        "parameters": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "dir_path": {"type": "string", "description": "..."}
          },
          "required": ["dir_path"]
        }
      }
    }
  ],
  "tool_choice": "auto"
}
```

**API鍝嶅簲鏍煎紡**锛?
```json
{
  "choices": [{
    "message": {
      "tool_calls": [{
        "id": "call_xxx",
        "type": "function",
        "function": {
          "name": "list_directory",
          "arguments": "{\"dir_path\": \"D:/\"}"
        }
      }]
    }
  }]
}
```

```python
def _get_default_allowed_paths() -> List[Path]:
    paths = [Path.home(), Path("/tmp"), Path("/var/tmp")]
    if os.name == 'nt':
        for letter in 'ABCDEFGHIJ':
            drive = Path(f"{letter}:/")
            if drive.exists():
                paths.append(drive)
    return paths
```

### 1.6 璺緞楠岃瘉鏀硅繘

```python
def _validate_path(self, file_path: str) -> tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:
    real_path = Path(os.path.realpath(os.path.expanduser(file_path)))
    for allowed in self.allowed_paths:
        allowed_real = Path(os.path.realpath(allowed))
        if str(real_path).startswith(str(allowed_real)):
            return True, None
    return False, f"璺緞 '{file_path}' 涓嶅湪鍏佽鐨勬搷浣滆寖鍥村唴..."
```

**鏀硅繘鐐?*锛?
1. 浣跨敤 `os.path.realpath` 瑙勮寖鍖栬矾寰?
2. 浣跨敤 `os.path.expanduser` 澶勭悊 `~`
3. 浣跨敤鍓嶇紑鍖归厤鑰岄潪绮剧‘鍖归厤

### 1.7 search_files瀹夊叏婕忔礊淇锛圥0锛?

**闂**锛氬師浠ｇ爜涓彧鏈?`search_files` 娌℃湁璺緞楠岃瘉锛岃繖鏄弗閲嶇殑瀹夊叏婕忔礊

**淇**锛?
```python
async def search_files(self, pattern: str, path: str = ".", ...):
    # 銆愬畨鍏ㄤ慨澶嶃€戦獙璇佹悳绱㈣矾寰?
    is_valid, error_msg = self._validate_path(path)
    if not is_valid:
        return _to_unified_format({
            "success": False,
            "error": error_msg,
            "matches": []
        }, "search_files")
```

### 1.9 澧炲己鐗圫ystem Prompt

**鍙傛暟鍛藉悕瑙勫垯锛堝叏灞€绾︽潫锛?*锛?
```
銆怚MPORTANT銆慞arameter Naming Rules - MUST follow these exactly:
- list_directory 鈫?use dir_path (NOT directory_path, NOT path)
- read_file 鈫?use file_path (NOT filepath, NOT path)
- write_file 鈫?use file_path (NOT filepath, NOT path)
- delete_file 鈫?use file_path (NOT filepath, NOT path)
- move_file 鈫?use source_path AND destination_path (NOT src, NOT dst)
- search_files 鈫?use pattern AND path

銆怓ORBIDDEN parameter names - DO NOT use銆?
- 鉂?directory_path (correct: dir_path)
- 鉂?filepath (correct: file_path)
- 鉂?src / source (correct: source_path)
- 鉂?dst / dest / destination (correct: destination_path)
```

        "source_path": "C:/old/file.txt",      // 鉁?CORRECT

    }
}
// 鉂?WRONG: {"src": "...", "dst": "..."}

## 1. 淇chat_stream()鏂规硶429閿欒澶勭悊 - 灏忔矆-2026-03-29

### 1.1 闂鑳屾櫙

鐢ㄦ埛楠屾敹鍙戠幇锛氬綋429闄愭祦鍙戠敓鏃讹紝TextStrategy杩斿洖绌哄唴瀹癸紝閿欒鎻愮ず娌℃湁鏄剧ず銆?
### 1.2 闂鏍瑰洜

鍦?`llm_core.py` 鐨?`chat_stream()` 鏂规硶涓紝褰?HTTP 鐘舵€佺爜涓嶆槸 200 鏃讹紙绗?67-169琛岋級锛?```python
if response.status_code != 200:
    yield StreamChunk(content="", model=self.model, is_done=True)
    return
```

**闂**锛氭病鏈変粠鍝嶅簲浣撲腑鎻愬彇閿欒淇℃伅骞惰缃?`stream_error`锛?
### 1.3 淇鍐呭

**淇敼鏂囦欢**: `backend/app/services/llm_core.py`

鍦?`response.status_code != 200` 鏃讹紝浠庡搷搴斾綋涓彁鍙栭敊璇俊鎭細
```python
if response.status_code != 200:
    error_body = ""
    try:
        error_body = await response.aread()
        error_text = error_body.decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
        logger.error(f"[chat_stream] HTTP {response.status_code} error response: {error_text[:500]}")
        try:
            error_json = json.loads(error_text)
            error_msg = error_json.get("error", {}).get("message", "")
            if error_msg:
                yield StreamChunk(content="", model=self.model, is_done=True, 
                    stream_error=f"API Error: {response.status_code}, {error_msg}",
                    stream_error_type="api_error")
                return
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            pass
        yield StreamChunk(content="", model=self.model, is_done=True,
            stream_error=f"HTTP {response.status_code}: {error_text[:200]}",
            stream_error_type="http_error")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"[chat_stream] Failed to read error response: {e}")
        yield StreamChunk(content="", model=self.model, is_done=True,
            stream_error=f"HTTP {response.status_code} error",
            stream_error_type="http_error")
    return
```

### 1.3 淇鍐呭

鍦?`_extract_from_text()` 鏂规硶鏈熬娣诲姞瀵规€荤粨鎬ф枃鏈殑妫€娴嬶細

```python
# 銆愪慨澶?2026-03-29銆戝鐞?LLM 杩斿洖绾枃鏈紙濡?"I will now summarize..."锛夌殑鎯呭喌

summarize_patterns = [
    r'(?:summarize|summary|鎬荤粨|I have found|I will)',
    r'(?:宸插畬鎴恷浠诲姟瀹屾垚|瀹屾垚浜?',
    r'(?:鏍规嵁.*?缁撴灉|鍩轰簬.*?鍐呭)',
]

        result["action"] = "finish"
        result["action_input"] = {}
        return result
```

```python
def _get_default_allowed_paths() -> List[Path]:
    paths = [Path.home(), Path("/tmp"), Path("/var/tmp")]
    if os.name == 'nt':
        for letter in 'ABCDEFGHIJ':
            drive = Path(f"{letter}:/")
            if drive.exists():
                paths.append(drive)
    return paths
```

### 1.6 璺緞楠岃瘉鏀硅繘

```python
def _validate_path(self, file_path: str) -> tuple[bool, Optional[str]]:
    real_path = Path(os.path.realpath(os.path.expanduser(file_path)))
    for allowed in self.allowed_paths:
        allowed_real = Path(os.path.realpath(allowed))
        if str(real_path).startswith(str(allowed_real)):
            return True, None
    return False, f"璺緞 '{file_path}' 涓嶅湪鍏佽鐨勬搷浣滆寖鍥村唴..."
```

**鏀硅繘鐐?*锛?1. 浣跨敤 `os.path.realpath` 瑙勮寖鍖栬矾寰?2. 浣跨敤 `os.path.expanduser` 澶勭悊 `~`
3. 浣跨敤鍓嶇紑鍖归厤鑰岄潪绮剧‘鍖归厤

### 1.9 澧炲己鐗圫ystem Prompt

**鍙傛暟鍛藉悕瑙勫垯锛堝叏灞€绾︽潫锛?*锛?```
銆怚MPORTANT銆慞arameter Naming Rules - MUST follow these exactly:
- list_directory 鈫?use dir_path (NOT directory_path, NOT path)
- read_file 鈫?use file_path (NOT filepath, NOT path)
- write_file 鈫?use file_path (NOT filepath, NOT path)
- delete_file 鈫?use file_path (NOT filepath, NOT path)
- move_file 鈫?use source_path AND destination_path (NOT src, NOT dst)
- search_files 鈫?use pattern AND path

銆怓ORBIDDEN parameter names - DO NOT use銆?
- 鉂?directory_path (correct: dir_path)
- 鉂?filepath (correct: file_path)
- 鉂?src / source (correct: source_path)
- 鉂?dst / dest / destination (correct: destination_path)
```

**Tool Call Examples锛?涓畬鏁寸ず渚嬶級**锛?```json
Example 1: List directory
{
    "thought": "User wants to see files in D drive root",
    "action": "list_directory",
    "action_input": {
        "dir_path": "D:/"  // 鉁?CORRECT: uses dir_path
    }
}
// 鉂?WRONG: {"directory_path": "D:/"} or {"path": "D:/"}

Example 2: Read file
{
    "action": "read_file",
    "action_input": {
        "file_path": "C:/Users/username/config.json"  // 鉁?CORRECT
    }
}

Example 3: Search files
{
    "action": "search_files",
    "action_input": {
        "pattern": "TODO",
        "path": "D:/project",
        "file_pattern": "*.py"
    }
}

Example 4: Move file
{
    "action": "move_file",
    "action_input": {
        "source_path": "C:/old/file.txt",      // 鉁?CORRECT
        "destination_path": "D:/new/file.txt"   // 鉁?CORRECT
    }
}
// 鉂?WRONG: {"src": "...", "dst": "..."}
```
